df4 = nation[['N_COMMENT', 'N_REGIONKEY']]
df5 = nation[['N_NAME', 'N_REGIONKEY', 'N_NATIONKEY', 'N_COMMENT']]
df6 = region.merge(df5, left_on='R_REGIONKEY', right_on='N_REGIONKEY')
df7 = df4.merge(df6, left_on='N_REGIONKEY', right_on='R_REGIONKEY')
df8 = df3.merge(df7, left_on='R_REGIONKEY', right_on='N_REGIONKEY')
df9 = nation[(nation['N_REGIONKEY'] <= 0) | (nation['N_REGIONKEY'] == 3)]
df10 = df8.merge(df9, left_on='R_REGIONKEY', right_on='N_REGIONKEY')
df11 = df10.groupby(by=['R_COMMENT', 'R_NAME']).agg('min', numeric_only=True)

df1 = part[['PT_COMMENT', 'MFGR', 'TYPE', 'SIZE', 'P_PARTKEY']]
df2 = df1.groupby(by=['SIZE', 'TYPE']).agg('count')

df1 = part[['P_NAME', 'RETAILPRICE', 'P_PARTKEY', 'CONTAINER']]
df2 = partsupp[['PS_SUPPKEY', 'AVAILQTY', 'P_COMMENT']]
df3 = supplier[(supplier['S_NATIONKEY'] < 19) & (supplier['S_SUPPKEY'] > 136) & (supplier['S_ACCTBAL'] >= 522.9868781450396)]
df4 = df3[['S_NATIONKEY', 'S_ADDRESS', 'S_PHONE', 'S_COMMENT', 'S_NAME']]
df5 = nation[(nation['N_REGIONKEY'] <= 2)]
df6 = df5[['N_NAME', 'N_REGIONKEY']]
df7 = df4.merge(df6, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df8 = df2.merge(df7, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df9 = supplier[(supplier['S_COMMENT'] == 'k') | (supplier['S_SUPPKEY'] > 8) & (supplier['S_COMMENT'] == '.') | (supplier['S_ACCTBAL'] == 1282.6586363691647)]
df10 = df9[['S_ADDRESS', 'S_PHONE', 'S_COMMENT', 'S_NATIONKEY']]
df11 = nation[(nation['N_COMMENT'].str.startswith(' ')) | (nation['N_NAME'] == 'R')]
df12 = df11[['N_NAME', 'N_NATIONKEY']]
df13 = df10.merge(df12, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df14 = df8.merge(df13, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df15 = df1.merge(df14, left_on='P_PARTKEY', right_on='PS_PARTKEY')
df16 = partsupp[['PS_SUPPKEY', 'P_COMMENT', 'SUPPLYCOST', 'AVAILQTY']]
df17 = df15.merge(df16, left_on='P_PARTKEY', right_on='PS_PARTKEY')
df18 = partsupp[(partsupp['PS_SUPPKEY'] < 3278) & (partsupp['PS_SUPPKEY'] < 4978)]
df19 = df18.merge(df18, left_on='PS_PARTKEY', right_on='P_PARTKEY')
df20 = supplier[(supplier['S_NATIONKEY'] > 14) & (supplier['S_ADDRESS'].str.startswith('g')) & (supplier['S_ACCTBAL'] <= 6401.16411254522) & (supplier['S_NAME'].str.startswith('S'))]
df21 = df20[['S_ADDRESS', 'S_NAME', 'S_ACCTBAL', 'S_NATIONKEY', 'S_SUPPKEY']]
df22 = nation[(nation['N_NAME'] != 'A') | (nation['N_COMMENT'] == 't')]
df23 = df22[['N_REGIONKEY', 'N_COMMENT', 'N_NATIONKEY', 'N_NAME']]
df24 = df21.merge(df23, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df25 = df19.merge(df24, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df26 = df17.merge(df25, left_on='P_PARTKEY', right_on='PS_PARTKEY')
df27 = df26.groupby(by=['CONTAINER']).agg('count')
